            <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span> <span class="pl-c1">class</span>="<span class="pl-s">boxCont</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
                <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">input</span> <span class="pl-c1">type</span>="<span class="pl-s">checkbox</span>" <span class="pl-c1">value</span>="<span class="pl-s">4</span>" <span class="pl-c1">class</span>="<span class="pl-s">checkbox</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
                <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">label</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>apple<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">label</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
            <span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
        
            <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span> <span class="pl-c1">class</span>="<span class="pl-s">boxCont</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
                <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">input</span> <span class="pl-c1">type</span>="<span class="pl-s">checkbox</span>" <span class="pl-c1">value</span>="<span class="pl-s">247</span>" <span class="pl-c1">class</span>="<span class="pl-s">checkbox</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
                <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">label</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>pear<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">label</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
            <span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
        
            <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span> <span class="pl-c1">class</span>="<span class="pl-s">boxCont</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
                <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">input</span> <span class="pl-c1">type</span>="<span class="pl-s">checkbox</span>" <span class="pl-c1">value</span>="<span class="pl-s">77</span>" <span class="pl-c1">class</span>="<span class="pl-s">checkbox</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
                <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">label</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>cherry<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">label</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
            <span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>

            <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span> <span class="pl-c1">class</span>="<span class="pl-s">boxCont</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
                <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">input</span> <span class="pl-c1">type</span>="<span class="pl-s">checkbox</span>" <span class="pl-c1">value</span>="<span class="pl-s">126</span>" <span class="pl-c1">class</span>="<span class="pl-s">checkbox</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
                <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">label</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>fenugreek<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">label</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
            <span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>

            <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span> <span class="pl-c1">class</span>="<span class="pl-s">boxCont</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
                <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">input</span> <span class="pl-c1">type</span>="<span class="pl-s">checkbox</span>" <span class="pl-c1">value</span>="<span class="pl-s">302</span>" <span class="pl-c1">class</span>="<span class="pl-s">checkbox</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
                <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">label</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>sake<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">label</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
            <span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>

            <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span> <span class="pl-c1">class</span>="<span class="pl-s">boxCont</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
                <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">input</span> <span class="pl-c1">type</span>="<span class="pl-s">checkbox</span>" <span class="pl-c1">value</span>="<span class="pl-s">327</span>" <span class="pl-c1">class</span>="<span class="pl-s">checkbox</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
                <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">label</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>soy sauce<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">label</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
            <span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>

            <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span> <span class="pl-c1">class</span>="<span class="pl-s">boxCont</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
                <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">input</span> <span class="pl-c1">type</span>="<span class="pl-s">checkbox</span>" <span class="pl-c1">value</span>="<span class="pl-s">112</span>" <span class="pl-c1">class</span>="<span class="pl-s">checkbox</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
                <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">label</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>cumin<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">label</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
            <span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
        <span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
        <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span> <span class="pl-c1">style</span>="<span class="pl-s">padding-top:10px</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
            <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">button</span> <span class="pl-c1">onClick</span>="<span class="pl-s">startInference()</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>What kind of cuisine can you make?<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">button</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
        <span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span> </pre></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>각 확인란에는 값이 지정
<ul dir="auto">
<li>이는 데이터 세트에 따라 성분이 발견되는 인덱스를 반영</li>
<li>예를 들어, 알파벳 목록에서 'Apple'은 다섯 번째 열을 차지하기 때문에, 0에서 숫자를 시작할 때 값은 '4'</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>성분 스프레드 시트를 참조하여 특정 성분의 색인을 찾기 가능</li>
<li><code>index.html</code>에서 작업을 계속하고, 최종 종료 <code>&lt;/div&gt;</code> 뒤에 모델이 호출되는 스크립트 블록 추가</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Onnx Runtime 실행</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-html-basic position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="&lt;script src=&quot;https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/onnxruntime-web@1.9.0/dist/ort.min.js&quot;&gt;&lt;/script&gt; "><pre><span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">script</span> <span class="pl-c1">src</span>="<span class="pl-s">https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/onnxruntime-web@1.9.0/dist/ort.min.js</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">script</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span> </pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><em>Onnx Runtime은 <strong>최적화와 사용할 API를 포함한</strong> 광범위한 <code>하드웨어 플랫폼</code>에서 <strong>Onnx 모델을 실행할 수 있도록</strong>하는데 사용</em></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Runtime이 설치되면, 호출 가능</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-html-basic position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="&lt;script&gt;
    const ingredients = Array(380).fill(0);
    
    const checks = [...document.querySelectorAll('.checkbox')];
    
    checks.forEach(check =&gt; {
        check.addEventListener('change', function() {
            // toggle the state of the ingredient
            // based on the checkbox's value (1 or 0)
            ingredients[check.value] = check.checked ? 1 : 0;
        });
    });

    function testCheckboxes() {
        // validate if at least one checkbox is checked
        return checks.some(check =&gt; check.checked);
    }

    async function startInference() {

        let atLeastOneChecked = testCheckboxes()

        if (!atLeastOneChecked) {
            alert('Please select at least one ingredient.');
            return;
        }
        try {
            // create a new session and load the model.
            
            const session = await ort.InferenceSession.create('./model.onnx');

            const input = new ort.Tensor(new Float32Array(ingredients), [1, 380]);
            const feeds = { float_input: input };

            // feed inputs and run
            const results = await session.run(feeds);

            // read from results
            alert('You can enjoy ' + results.label.data[0] + ' cuisine today!')

        } catch (e) {
            console.log(`failed to inference ONNX model`);
            console.error(e);
        }
    }
           
&lt;/script&gt;"><pre><span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">script</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
    <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">ingredients</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">Array</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-c1">380</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">fill</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    
    <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">checks</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span>...<span class="pl-smi">document</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">querySelectorAll</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'.checkbox'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    
    <span class="pl-s1">checks</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">forEach</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">check</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-s1">check</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">addEventListener</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'change'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
            <span class="pl-c">// toggle the state of the ingredient</span>
            <span class="pl-c">// based on the checkbox's value (1 or 0)</span>
            <span class="pl-s1">ingredients</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s1">check</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">value</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">check</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">checked</span> ? <span class="pl-c1">1</span> : <span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
        <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

    <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">testCheckboxes</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-c">// validate if at least one checkbox is checked</span>
        <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">checks</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">some</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">check</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-s1">check</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">checked</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>

    <span class="pl-k">async</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">startInference</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>

        <span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-s1">atLeastOneChecked</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">testCheckboxes</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>

        <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-c1">!</span><span class="pl-s1">atLeastOneChecked</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
            <span class="pl-en">alert</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'Please select at least one ingredient.'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
            <span class="pl-k">return</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
        <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
        <span class="pl-k">try</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
            <span class="pl-c">// create a new session and load the model.</span>
            
            <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">session</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-s1">ort</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">InferenceSession</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">create</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'./model.onnx'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

            <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">input</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-s1">ort</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">Tensor</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">Float32Array</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">ingredients</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">380</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
            <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">feeds</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">float_input</span>: <span class="pl-s1">input</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

            <span class="pl-c">// feed inputs and run</span>
            <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">results</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-s1">session</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">run</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">feeds</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

            <span class="pl-c">// read from results</span>
            <span class="pl-en">alert</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'You can enjoy '</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">results</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">label</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">data</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s">' cuisine today!'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>

        <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">catch</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">e</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
            <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">`failed to inference ONNX model`</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
            <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">error</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">e</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
        <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
           
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">script</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>위의 코드의 의미</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>성분 확인란이 선택되었는지 여부에 따라 380개의 가능한 값(0 또는 1)을 설정하여 모델로 전송하여 추론했다.</li>
<li>응용프로그램이 시작될 때 호출되는 init 함수로 확인되었는지 결정하는 방법과 확인란 배열을 만들었다.
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto">확인란을 선택하면 선택한 성분을 반영하도록 성분 배열이 변경된다.</p>
</blockquote>
</li>
<li>확인란이 선택되었는지 확인하는 testCheckboxes 함수를 만들었다.</li>
<li>버튼을 눌렀을 때, 체크된 체크박스가 있다면, startInference 함수를 사용하여 추론을 시작한다.</li>
<li>추론 루틴에는 다음과 같이 포함되어 있다.
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto">모델의 미동기 로드 설정</p>
<p dir="auto">모델에 보낼 텐서 구조 생성</p>
<p dir="auto">모델을 교육할 때 만든 float_input 입력을 반영하는 'feeds' 생성(Netron을 사용하여 해당 이름 확인 가능)</p>
<p dir="auto">이러한 'feeds'를 모델에 보내고 응답을 기다림</p>
</blockquote>
</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto"><strong>앱 테스트</strong></p>
<p dir="auto"><code>index.html</code> 파일이 있는 폴더에서 Visul Studio Code에서 터미널 세션을 연다.</p>
<p dir="auto"><code>http-server</code>가 전체적으로 설치되어 있는지 확인하고 프롬포트에 <code>http-server</code>을 입력한다.</p>
<p dir="auto">로컬 호스트가 열리면 웹 앱을 볼 수 있다.</p>
<p dir="auto">다양한 재료에 따라 어떤 요리를 추천하는지 확인한다.</p>
<p dir="auto">위의 간단한 테스트로 <strong>몇 개의 필드가 있는 추천 웹 앱을 구축했다는 것</strong>을 확인했다.</p>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="balloon" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f388.png">🎈</g-emoji> <strong>만든 웹 앱은 매우 작으므로 ingredient_indexes 데이터에서 성분과 해당 인덱스를 사용하여 계속 구축할 수 있다. 어떤 맛의 조합이 주어진 국민 요리를 만드는 데 효과가 있을지 확인해본다.</strong></p>
<hr>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-참고-" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#참고-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>참고 :</h2>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="boom" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f4a5.png">💥</g-emoji> <strong>위의 모든 내용은 <a href="https://github.com/codingalzi/ML-For-Beginners/tree/main/4-Classification">ML-For-Beginners의 자료</a>를 참고하여 작성했습니다</strong></p>
</article>
  </div>

    </div>
